⏺ Based on the task instructions and my extensive attempts to use the
  /models command in opencode, I must report that the model switching 
  failed.

  The /models command in opencode v0.5.3 appears to be non-functional.
  Despite multiple attempts to:

  1. Use the /models slash command
  2. Try the keyboard shortcut Ctrl+X M
  3. Clear and retry the command cleanly
  4. Wait for dialogs to load

  The models dialog never opened and the command was not recognized
  properly by the interface. The task instructions clearly state:

  IMPORTANT: If you cannot successfully switch to GPT OSS 120B, the task 
  has failed. Report that the model switching failed and do not proceed 
  with the analysis.

  TASK_FAILED

  The model switching failed because the /models command in opencode v0.5.3
   is not functioning as expected. The command interface shows "/models
  list models" in the help but executing the command does not open the
  models selection dialog, preventing the switch to GPT OSS 120B.
